 The Center has revoked the citizenship of Telangana MLA Ramesh Chennamaneni
 samachar agency pitiai ne is baat kii jaankaree di he
 The Center stated that the MLA is a German citizen and he fraudulently obtained Indian citizenship
 centre ne kaha ki rajya kii sattarudh telugana raashtra samiti (tiares) ke sadsy chennamaneni ne apane videsh daure ke bare main tathy chhupaae hai

 ) In the midst of efforts to send humans to Mars by 2030, NASA today launched 'insight'
 america antariksh agency nasa ne mangal grah ke rahasy kaa adhyayan ke liye mars lander 'insite' ko launch kiya he
 It was successfully launched from the Vandenberg Air Force Base in California at 4:35 pm Indian time (07:05 AM US time)
 nasa kii yah pariyojna 99
 3 million dollars, which aims to increase information about the internal conditions of Mars
 saath hi, laal grah par maanav ko bhejne se pehle vahaan kii paristhitiyon kaa pataa lagaana or prithvi jaise chattani grahon ke nirmaan kii prakriya ko samajhnaa he
 If everything goes according to plan, the lander will land on the surface of Mars on 26 November
 ‘insite’ kaa puraa naam ‘interior exploration ujing cesmik investigations’ he
 NASA Chief Scientist Jim Green said that experts already know that there have been earthquakes, landslides and hit meteorites on Mars
 green ne kaha ki lekin mangal bukamp kaa saamana karne main kitna sakasham he? hamen jaanane kii jarurat he
 The main instrument on the spacecraft is the seismometer, which is designed by the French Space Agency
 lander ke mangal kii sataha par utarane ke baad ek ‘robotic arm’ sataha par cesmometer (bukampamapi upkaran) lagayegaa
 The second key tool is a 'self hammering' probe that will monitor the flow of heat across the planet's surface
 nasa ne kaha ki jaanch ke tahat sataha par 10 se 16 foot gaharaa suraakh kiya jayega
 It will be 15 times deeper than previous Mars missions
 darasal, 2030 tak mangal par logon ko bhejne kii nasa kii koshishon ke liye ‘laal grah’ ke taapmaana ko samajhnaa mahatvapurn he
 The lander, which uses solar energy and battery power, is designed to operate for 26 months
 nasa ke jet propalshan laboratory ke insite prabandhak tom hoyman ne bataaya ki aashaa he ki yah isse adhik samay tak chalegaa
 Insight will be nasa's first lander to land there since Curiosity Rover landed on Mars in 2012
 is project par kareeb 99
 It is said to have cost 30 million dollars
 yah mangal par sthitiyon ke bare main pataa lagane ke alaava is baat kaa pataa lagayegaa ki arabon varsh pehle kaise vahaan dharti kii tarah patharilaa grah bana
 If all goes well, the lander will start functioning on the Red Planet by 26 November
 milinium city yaa alumunium city naam rakh dene se kuch khaas nahin badal jaataa
 When the structure of the roads has not changed, how will the mind's mind change
 gudgaanv naamak atipracheen or uttar aadhunik nagar vyavastha se sata ek gaanv he chakarpur
 We and you have been studying since the time of Baba Adam that the soul of India lives in the villages
 ab yah vivaad kaa vishay he ki kya sari atmaaen gaanvon main rahati hai yaa unamem se kuch nagaron, mahanagaron or smart nagaron main bhi rahati hai
 The soul of the soul residing in the villages is of divine level or some of the souls in them also have character
 hua yun ki bina kisi khel mantri yaa khel vibhaag ke gudgaanv ke chakarpur gaanv kii team ne ek kabddi kii pratiyogita kaa aayojan kiya
 40 teams from nearby districts and villages came here
 pratham vijeta team ke liye 21,000 kii inaam raashi rakhi gai
 a prize money of 11,000 was placed for the second winning team
 pratiyogita main shaamil hone kii koi fees nahin thi
 The team's name was Lala Raju Chakarpur team, where this competition was being organized
 gadhe nile rang kii jersey vaali is team ke captain lala urf raju hai jo dalit hai
 His team also includes Jat players who belonged to another village
 lala ne chaar jat khilaadiyon ko panipat se khilne ke liye bulaayaa tha
 Raju, Deepak and Ajay were all three Dalit players
 yah acchhee baat he ki dalit captain kii team main jat khilaadi duusare jile se khilne aa gaye
 But all the players of the team they met were Yadavs, who came from the nearby village of Sikanderpur
 gram chakarpur, din 15 agast
 Kabaddi Kabaddi Kabaddi
 ek taraf daliton kii team, duusari taraf yadavon kii team
 Kabaddi Kabaddi Kabaddi Kabaddi, 32-1 team of Dalits got ahead
 kabddi kabddi kabddi kabddi, yadavon kii team daliton kii team se haar gai
 Kabaddi Kabaddi Kabaddi, one team could not bear the shock of defeat, the team of Dalits got attacked
 lathi, chad se hamalaa hua, marpet bhi hone lagi
 Abuses were started in the name of caste
 5 dalit khilaadi ghayal ho gaye
 It is alleged that the defeat was so great that Yadav players of Sikanderpur were not tolerated
 unke saath vahaan maujuud darshakon main unki jati ke log bhi gusse main aa gaye
 Even in the middle village, they could not bear the shameful defeat at the hands of Dalit players
 chakkarpur kii aabaadi paanch hazaar ke kareeb he
 There are three thousand Yadavs and about two thousand Dalits
 gaanv kii team gaanv main pit gai or gaanv ke log chupchaap dekhte rahe
 It is also important to know the answer to this question, whether the remaining four Jat players were also victims of his violence when the mob was killing the Dalit players or the mob left them
 philhal yah maamla gudgaanv ke sector 29 ke thane main darj he or police jaanch kar rahi he
 Our colleague Sushil Kumar Mohapatra has spoken to these injured
 yogendra or vijendra donon hi bhai hai
 These two were not playing but watching
 donon hi dalit hai
 They came to support their team
 captain ke haath main chot ai he
 The angry mob also picked up and threw away Vijendra's eight-year-old son
 bete kii haalat thik he lekin wo aspataal main pita ke saath hi he
 Listen to this child, even if caste is not the reason for this violence, how are we giving so much relaxation to any crowd who does not care about anyone
 aath saal ke bachche ko uthaakar phenkane kaa dussahas kisi bheed ko sankhya se aata he yaa jati ke ahankaar se bhi aata he
 Was the anger due to defeat or was he unable to digest due to the defeat of Dalits
 zaruri he ki ham samaaj ke bheetar baithi is sankramak beemaari kii pahchaan jad se karen
 The competition was started to increase mutual unity among the castes
 lekin kisi ko nahin pataa tha ki ek aisi team jeet jaaegi jiske zyaadaatar khilaadi dalit the
 Injured player Yogendra told Sushil that the players of Sunderpur have been doing this already
 unhone is team ko bulaayaa bhi nahin, isliye bhi gussa tha
 Even the players are sad that they are not supported by the people of their village
 baahar ke gaanv vaale maarthe pitate rahe, lekin apano ne madad nahin kii
 If we are unable to bear the success of any Dalit captain at the village level, then by tweeting at the Olympics, the medal is not going to come
 daliton ke prati hinsa ek maansikta he
 Dalits have been the victims of upper caste and backward caste violence in turn
 ye kahani ek or kahani bataati he
 That story is a bit good that even today in many areas of the country people organize sports competitions at their level
 chakkarpur kii kabddi pehali baar ho rahi thi or 40 timen bhaag lene aa gayi
 This means that the spirit of the game may not be visible in the Olpink but the village is seen in the streets
 tippaniyan In Jharkhand, swimming pools costing crores have been closed for months, but swimmers of the state are practicing in streams, pits
 yah tasviir is baat kaa pramaan he ki hamaare khilaadiyon main yaa janata main khel ke prati jazbaa china yaa japan se kam nahin he
 Players practice hours in Kanke's check dam adjacent to Ranchi
 jaan par khelkar un anjaan jagahon par ghota lagane kii ye tasviren hamaari ankhon ko tabhi kyon chubhti hai jab koi deepa karmakar padak pate pate rah jaati he
 All the officials and sports ministers have also gone to see what they have done about their sports in the countries of the world
 kaash ve hindustan ke gaanvon main gum aate to kam se kam junun dikh jaataa
 If these swimmers win the medal tomorrow, then who will be the leader who will not tweet
 magar baat netaa kii bhi nahin he
 It is a matter that swimming pools worth crores of rupees have been built
 jab he tab kyon nahin in tairaakon ke liye uplabdh hai
 Whose failure is this jharkhand kii ghatana kaa gudgaanv kii ghatana se koi taalluk nahin he, sirf itnaa sambandh he ki vyavastha nahin he magar log khel ko zindaa rakhe hue hai
 What happened as the media reported, ie the clash took place on caste or there might have been some other reasons
 chakarpur jahaan is pratiyogita kaa aayojan ho rahaa tha uski team kaa naam tha lala raju chakarpur team
 The team with a thick blue jersey is captain Lala alias Raju who is a Dalit
 unki team main jat khilaadi bhi hai jo duusare gaanv ke the
 Lala had invited four Jat players to play from Panipat
 raju, deepak or ajay ye teenon dalit khilaadi the
 It is a good thing that Jat players in Dalit captain's team came from other district to play
 lekin inkaa muqabla jis team se hua uske sabhi khilaadi yadav the, jo paas ke gaanv sikandarpur se aae the
 Village Chakarpur, day 15 August kabddi kabddi kabddi kabddi
 On one side, the Dalits team, on the other side the Yadavs team
 kabddi kabddi kabddi kabddi, 32-1 se daliton kii team aage nikal gai
 Kabaddi Kabaddi Kabaddi Kabaddi, the team of Yadavs lost to the team of Dalits
 kabddi kabddi kabddi kabddi, haar kaa sadma ek team bardaasht nahin kar pai, daliton kii team par hamalaa ho gaya
 Attacked with sticks, sticks, also started fighting
 jati ke naam se gaaliyaan di jane lageen
 5 Dalit players were injured
 aarope he ki haar itani badi thi ki sikandarpur ke yadav khilaadiyon ko bardaasht nahin hua
 People of his caste got angry in the audience present there with him
 dalit khilaadiyon ke haathon sharmnaak haar wo bhi bich gaanv main bardaasht nahin kar sake
 Chakpur has a population of around five thousand
 teen hazaar yadav hai or kareeb do hazaar dalit
 The village team was beaten in the village and the people of the village kept watching silently
 is sawaal kaa jawaab jaananaa bhi zaruri he ki kya jab bheed dalit khilaadiyon ko maar rahi thi tab baaki ke chaar jat khilaadi bhi uski hinsa ke shikaar hue yaa bheed ne unhen chhod diya
 At present, this case is registered in the Sector 29 police station of Gurgaon and the police is investigating
 hamaare sahyogi susheel kumaar mahapatra ne in ghayalon se baat kii he
 Both Yogendra and Vijendra are brothers
 ye donon khel nahin rahe the balki dekh rahe the
 Both are Dalits
 ye apni team ko saport karne aae the
 The captain has suffered an injury
 gussai bheed ne vijendra ke aath saal ke bete ko bhi uthaakar phenk diya
 The son's condition is fine but he is with the father in the hospital
 is bachche ko suniye, agar is hinsa main jati kaaran nahin bhi he to bhi ham baat baat main kisi bhi bheed ko itani chhot kaise de rahe hai jo kisi kii parvaah nahin karti he
 The courage to pick up and throw an eight-year-old child comes from a crowd or from the arrogance of caste
 kya gussa haar ke kaaran hi tha yaa daliton se haar jane ke kaaran wo pachaa nahin paae

 pratiyogita shuru hui tha ki jatiyon ke bich aapasi ekta bade

 ghayal khilaadi yogendra ne susheel ko bataaya ki sundarpur ke khilaadi pehle se aisa karte rahe hai
 He did not even call this team, so was angry
 yahaan tak ki khilaadiyon ko is baat kaa dukh bhi he ki unhen apane gaanv ke logon ne saport nahin kiya
 The villagers from outside kept beating, but their own did not help
 ham gaanv ke str par kisi dalit captain kii kamyaabi bardaasht nahin kar pate hai to olympic main keval twit karne se to medal nahin aane vaala he
 Violence towards Dalits is a mindset
